    40	const (
    41	        // keep the enqueue period a smaller value to make sure the BSL can be validated as expected.
    42	        // The BSL validation frequency is 1 minute by default, if we set the enqueue period as 1 minute,
    43	        // this will cause the actual validation interval for each BSL to be 2 minutes
    44	        bslValidationEnqueuePeriod = 10 * time.Second
    45	)
    46

    81	func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
    82	        var unavailableErrors []string
    83	        var location velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
    84	
    85	        log := r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation).WithField(constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation, req.NamespacedName.String())
    86	        log.Debug("Validating availability of BackupStorageLocation")
    87	
    88	        locationList, err := storage.ListBackupStorageLocations(r.ctx, r.client, req.Namespace)
    89	        if err != nil {
    90	                log.WithError(err).Error("No BackupStorageLocations found, at least one is required")
    91	                return ctrl.Result{}, nil
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        pluginManager := r.newPluginManager(log)
    95	        defer pluginManager.CleanupClients()
    96	
    97	        // find the BSL that matches the request
    98	        for _, bsl := range locationList.Items {
    99	                if bsl.Name == req.Name && bsl.Namespace == req.Namespace {
   100	                        location = bsl
   101	                }
   102	        }
   103	
   104	        if location.Name == "" || location.Namespace == "" {
   105	                log.WithError(err).Error("BackupStorageLocation is not found")
   106	                return ctrl.Result{}, nil
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        // decide the default BSL
   110	        defaultFound, err := r.ensureSingleDefaultBSL(locationList)
   111	        if err != nil {
   112	                log.WithError(err).Error("failed to ensure single default bsl")
   113	                return ctrl.Result{}, nil
   114	        }
   115	
   116	        func() {
   117	                var err error
   118	                original := location.DeepCopy()
   119	                defer func() {
   120	                        location.Status.LastValidationTime = &metav1.Time{Time: time.Now().UTC()}
   121	                        if err != nil {
   122	                                log.Info("BackupStorageLocation is invalid, marking as unavailable")
   123	                                err = errors.Wrapf(err, "BackupStorageLocation %q is unavailable", location.Name)
   124	                                unavailableErrors = append(unavailableErrors, err.Error())
   125	                                location.Status.Phase = velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseUnavailable
   126	                                location.Status.Message = err.Error()
   127	                        } else {
   128	                                log.Info("BackupStorageLocations is valid, marking as available")
   129	                                location.Status.Phase = velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseAvailable
   130	                                location.Status.Message = ""
   131	                        }
   132	                        if err := r.client.Patch(r.ctx, &location, client.MergeFrom(original)); err != nil {
   133	                                log.WithError(err).Error("Error updating BackupStorageLocation phase")
   134	                        }
   135	                }()
   136	
   137	                backupStore, err := r.backupStoreGetter.Get(&location, pluginManager, log)
   138	                if err != nil {
   139	                        log.WithError(err).Error("Error getting a backup store")
   140	                        return
   141	                }
   142	
   143	                log.Info("Validating BackupStorageLocation")
   144	                err = backupStore.IsValid()
   145	                if err != nil {
   146	                        log.WithError(err).Error("fail to validate backup store")
   147	                        return
   148	                }
   149	        }()
   150	
   151	        r.logReconciledPhase(defaultFound, locationList, unavailableErrors)
   152	
   153	        return ctrl.Result{}, nil
   154	}
   155	
   156	func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) logReconciledPhase(defaultFound bool, locationList velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList, errs []string) {
   157	        var availableBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   158	        var unAvailableBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   159	        var unknownBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   160	        log := r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation)
   161	
   162	        for i, location := range locationList.Items {
   163	                phase := location.Status.Phase
   164	                switch phase {
   165	                case velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseAvailable:
   166	                        availableBSLs = append(availableBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
   167	                case velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseUnavailable:
   168	                        unAvailableBSLs = append(unAvailableBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
   169	                default:
   170	                        unknownBSLs = append(unknownBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
   171	                }
   172	        }
   173	
   174	        numAvailable := len(availableBSLs)
   175	        numUnavailable := len(unAvailableBSLs)
   176	        numUnknown := len(unknownBSLs)
   177	
   178	        if numUnavailable+numUnknown == len(locationList.Items) { // no available BSL
   179	                if len(errs) > 0 {
   180	                        log.Errorf("Current BackupStorageLocations available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v, %s)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown, strings.Join(errs, "; "))
   181	                } else {
   182	                        log.Errorf("Current BackupStorageLocations available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown)
   183	                }
   184	        } else if numUnavailable > 0 { // some but not all BSL unavailable
   185	                log.Warnf("Unavailable BackupStorageLocations detected: available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v, %s)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown, strings.Join(errs, "; "))
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        if !defaultFound {
   189	                log.Warn("There is no existing BackupStorageLocation set as default. Please see `velero backup-location -h` for options.")
   190	        }
   191	}
   192	
   193	func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
   194	        gp := kube.NewGenericEventPredicate(func(object client.Object) bool {
   195	                location := object.(*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation)
   196	                return storage.IsReadyToValidate(location.Spec.ValidationFrequency, location.Status.LastValidationTime, r.defaultBackupLocationInfo.ServerValidationFrequency, r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation))
   197	        })
   198	        g := kube.NewPeriodicalEnqueueSource(
   199	                r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation),
   200	                mgr.GetClient(),
   201	                &velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList{},
   202	                bslValidationEnqueuePeriod,
   203	                kube.PeriodicalEnqueueSourceOption{
   204	                        Predicates: []predicate.Predicate{gp},
   205	                },
   206	        )
   207	
   208	        return ctrl.NewControllerManagedBy(mgr).
   209	                // As the "status.LastValidationTime" field is always updated, this triggers new reconciling process, skip the update event that include no spec change to avoid the reconcile loop
   210	                For(&velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation{}, builder.WithPredicates(kube.SpecChangePredicate{})).
   211	                WatchesRawSource(g).
   212	                Named(constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation).
   213	                Complete(r)
   214	}
   215	
   216	// ensureSingleDefaultBSL ensures that there is only one default BSL in the namespace.
   217	// the default BSL priority is as follows:
   218	// 1. follow the user's setting (the most recent validation BSL is the default BSL)
   219	// 2. follow the server's setting ("velero server --default-backup-storage-location")
   220	func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) ensureSingleDefaultBSL(locationList velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList) (bool, error) {
   221	        // get all default BSLs
   222	        var defaultBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   223	        var defaultFound bool
   224	        for i, location := range locationList.Items {
   225	                if location.Spec.Default {
   226	                        defaultBSLs = append(defaultBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
   227	                }
   228	        }
   229	
   230	        if len(defaultBSLs) > 1 { // more than 1 default BSL
   231	                // find the most recent updated default BSL
   232	                var mostRecentCreatedBSL *velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   233	                defaultFound = true
   234	                for _, bsl := range defaultBSLs {
   235	                        if mostRecentCreatedBSL == nil {
   236	                                mostRecentCreatedBSL = bsl
   237	                                continue
   238	                        }
   239	                        // For lack of a better way to compare timestamps, we use the CreationTimestamp
   240	                        // it cloud not really find the most recent updated BSL, but it is good enough for now
   241	                        bslTimestamp := bsl.CreationTimestamp
   242	                        mostRecentTimestamp := mostRecentCreatedBSL.CreationTimestamp
   243	                        if mostRecentTimestamp.Before(&bslTimestamp) {
   244	                                mostRecentCreatedBSL = bsl
   245	                        }
   246	                }
   247	
   248	                // unset all other default BSLs
   249	                for _, bsl := range defaultBSLs {
   250	                        if bsl.Name != mostRecentCreatedBSL.Name {
   251	                                bsl.Spec.Default = false
   252	                                if err := r.client.Update(r.ctx, bsl); err != nil {
   253	                                        return defaultFound, errors.Wrapf(err, "failed to unset default backup storage location %q", bsl.Name)
   254	                                }
   255	                                r.log.Debugf("update default backup storage location %q to false", bsl.Name)
   256	                        }
   257	                }
   258	        } else if len(defaultBSLs) == 0 { // no default BSL
   259	                defaultFound = false
   260	        } else { // only 1 default BSL
   261	                defaultFound = true
   262	        }
   263	        return defaultFound, nil
   264	}

    46	var _ = Describe("Backup Storage Location Reconciler", func() {
    47	        It("Should successfully patch a backup storage location object status phase according to whether its storage is valid or not", func() {
    48	                tests := []struct {
    49	                        backupLocation    *velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
    50	                        isValidError      error
    51	                        expectedIsDefault bool
    52	                        expectedPhase     velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhase
    53	                }{
    54	                        {
    55	                                backupLocation:    builder.ForBackupStorageLocation("ns-1", "location-1").ValidationFrequency(1 * time.Second).Default(true).Result(),
    56	                                isValidError:      nil,
    57	                                expectedIsDefault: true,
    58	                                expectedPhase:     velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseAvailable,
    59	                        },
    60	                        {
    61	                                backupLocation:    builder.ForBackupStorageLocation("ns-1", "location-2").ValidationFrequency(1 * time.Second).Result(),
    62	                                isValidError:      errors.New("an error"),
    63	                                expectedIsDefault: false,
    64	                                expectedPhase:     velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseUnavailable,
    65	                        },
    66	                }
    67	
    68	                // Setup
    69	                var (
    70	                        pluginManager = &pluginmocks.Manager{}
    71	                        backupStores  = make(map[string]*persistencemocks.BackupStore)
    72	                )
    73	                pluginManager.On("CleanupClients").Return(nil)
    74	
    75	                locations := new(velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList)
    76	                for i, test := range tests {
    77	                        location := test.backupLocation
    78	                        locations.Items = append(locations.Items, *location)
    79	                        backupStores[location.Name] = &persistencemocks.BackupStore{}
    80	                        backupStore := backupStores[location.Name]
    81	                        backupStore.On("IsValid").Return(tests[i].isValidError)
    82	                }
    83	
    84	                // Setup reconciler
    85	                Expect(velerov1api.AddToScheme(scheme.Scheme)).To(Succeed())
    86	                r := backupStorageLocationReconciler{

    89	                        defaultBackupLocationInfo: storage.DefaultBackupLocationInfo{
    90	                                StorageLocation:           "location-1",
    91	                                ServerValidationFrequency: 0,
    92	                        },

    96	                }
    97

   100	                        actualResult, err := r.Reconcile(ctx, ctrl.Request{
   101	                                NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{Namespace: location.Namespace, Name: location.Name},
   102	                        })

   104	                        Expect(err).ToNot(HaveOccurred())

   107	                        instance := &velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation{}
   108	                        err = r.client.Get(ctx, key, instance)
   109	                        Expect(err).ToNot(HaveOccurred())
   110	                        Expect(instance.Spec.Default).To(BeIdenticalTo(tests[i].expectedIsDefault))
   111	                        Expect(instance.Status.Phase).To(BeIdenticalTo(tests[i].expectedPhase))
   112	                }

   180	func TestEnsureSingleDefaultBSL(t *testing.T) {
   181	        tests := []struct {
   182	                name               string
   183	                locations          velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList
   184	                defaultBackupInfo  storage.DefaultBackupLocationInfo
   185	                expectedDefaultSet bool
   186	                expectedError      error
   187	        }{
   188	                {
   189	                        name: "MultipleDefaults",
   190	                        locations: func() velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList {
   191	                                var locations velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList
   192	                                locations.Items = append(locations.Items, *builder.ForBackupStorageLocation(velerov1api.DefaultNamespace, "location-1").LastValidationTime(time.Now()).Default(true).Result())
   193	                                locations.Items = append(locations.Items, *builder.ForBackupStorageLocation(velerov1api.DefaultNamespace, "location-2").LastValidationTime(time.Now().Add(-1 * time.Hour)).Default(true).Result())
   194	                                return locations
   195	                        }(),
   196	                        expectedDefaultSet: true,
   197	                        expectedError:      nil,
   198	                },
   199	                {
   200	                        name: "NoDefault with exist default bsl in defaultBackupInfo",
   201	                        locations: func() velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList {
   202	                                var locations velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList
   203	                                locations.Items = append(locations.Items, *builder.ForBackupStorageLocation(velerov1api.DefaultNamespace, "location-1").Default(false).Result())
   204	                                locations.Items = append(locations.Items, *builder.ForBackupStorageLocation(velerov1api.DefaultNamespace, "location-2").Default(false).Result())
   205	                                return locations
   206	                        }(),
   207	                        defaultBackupInfo: storage.DefaultBackupLocationInfo{
   208	                                StorageLocation: "location-2",
   209	                        },
   210	                        expectedDefaultSet: false,
   211	                        expectedError:      nil,
   212	                },
   213	                {
   214	                        name: "NoDefault with non-exist default bsl in defaultBackupInfo",
   215	                        locations: func() velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList {
   216	                                var locations velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList
   217	                                locations.Items = append(locations.Items, *builder.ForBackupStorageLocation(velerov1api.DefaultNamespace, "location-1").Default(false).Result())
   218	                                locations.Items = append(locations.Items, *builder.ForBackupStorageLocation(velerov1api.DefaultNamespace, "location-2").Default(false).Result())
   219	                                return locations
   220	                        }(),
   221	                        defaultBackupInfo: storage.DefaultBackupLocationInfo{
   222	                                StorageLocation: "location-3",
   223	                        },
   224	                        expectedDefaultSet: false,
   225	                        expectedError:      nil,
   226	                },
   227	                {
   228	                        name: "SingleDefault",
   229	                        locations: func() velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList {
   230	                                var locations velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList
   231	                                locations.Items = append(locations.Items, *builder.ForBackupStorageLocation(velerov1api.DefaultNamespace, "location-1").Default(true).Result())
   232	                                locations.Items = append(locations.Items, *builder.ForBackupStorageLocation(velerov1api.DefaultNamespace, "location-2").Default(false).Result())
   233	                                return locations
   234	                        }(),
   235	                        expectedDefaultSet: true,
   236	                        expectedError:      nil,
   237	                },
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        for _, test := range tests {
   241	                // Setup reconciler
   242	                require.NoError(t, velerov1api.AddToScheme(scheme.Scheme))
   243	                t.Run(test.name, func(t *testing.T) {
   244	                        r := &backupStorageLocationReconciler{
   245	                                ctx:                       context.Background(),
   246	                                client:                    fake.NewClientBuilder().WithScheme(scheme.Scheme).WithRuntimeObjects(&test.locations).Build(),
   247	                                defaultBackupLocationInfo: test.defaultBackupInfo,
   248	                                log:                       velerotest.NewLogger(),
   249	                        }
   250	                        defaultFound, err := r.ensureSingleDefaultBSL(test.locations)
   251	
   252	                        assert.Equal(t, test.expectedDefaultSet, defaultFound)
   253	                        assert.Equal(t, test.expectedError, err)
   254	                })
   255	        }
   256	}
   257	
   258	func TestBSLReconcile(t *testing.T) {
   259	        tests := []struct {
   260	                name          string
   261	                locationList  velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList
   262	                defaultFound  bool
   263	                expectedError error
   264	        }{
   265	                {
   266	                        name:          "NoBSL",
   267	                        locationList:  velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList{},
   268	                        defaultFound:  false,
   269	                        expectedError: nil,
   270	                },
   271	                {
   272	                        name: "BSLNotFound",
   273	                        locationList: func() velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList {
   274	                                var locations velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList
   275	                                locations.Items = append(locations.Items, *builder.ForBackupStorageLocation(velerov1api.DefaultNamespace, "location-2").Result())
   276	                                return locations
   277	                        }(),
   278	                        defaultFound:  false,
   279	                        expectedError: nil,
   280	                },
   281	        }
   282	        pluginManager := &pluginmocks.Manager{}
   283	        pluginManager.On("CleanupClients").Return(nil)
   284	        for _, test := range tests {
   285	                // Setup reconciler
   286	                require.NoError(t, velerov1api.AddToScheme(scheme.Scheme))
   287	                t.Run(test.name, func(t *testing.T) {
   288	                        r := &backupStorageLocationReconciler{
   289	                                ctx:              context.Background(),
   290	                                client:           fake.NewClientBuilder().WithScheme(scheme.Scheme).WithRuntimeObjects(&test.locationList).Build(),
   291	                                newPluginManager: func(logrus.FieldLogger) clientmgmt.Manager { return pluginManager },
   292	                                log:              velerotest.NewLogger(),
   293	                        }
   294	
   295	                        result, err := r.Reconcile(context.TODO(), ctrl.Request{NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{Namespace: velerov1api.DefaultNamespace, Name: "location-1"}})
   296	                        assert.Equal(t, test.expectedError, err)
   297	                        assert.Equal(t, ctrl.Result{}, result)
   298	                })
   299	        }
   300	}

   152	                        return

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_bsl_controller_integration.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"time"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"
	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types"
	"k8s.io/client-go/kubernetes/scheme"
	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client/fake"

	"github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/internal/storage"
	velerov1api "github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pkg/apis/velero/v1"
	"github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pkg/builder"
	"github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pkg/controller"
	"github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pkg/metrics"
	persistencemocks "github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pkg/persistence/mocks"
	"github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pkg/plugin/clientmgmt"
	pluginmocks "github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pkg/plugin/mocks"
)

// NewFakeObjectBackupStoreGetter returns a fake ObjectBackupStoreGetter for tests.
func NewFakeObjectBackupStoreGetter(backupStores map[string]*persistencemocks.BackupStore) *FakeObjectBackupStoreGetter {
	return &FakeObjectBackupStoreGetter{
		backupStores: backupStores,
	}
}

type FakeObjectBackupStoreGetter struct {
	backupStores map[string]*persistencemocks.BackupStore
}

func (f *FakeObjectBackupStoreGetter) Get(location *velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation, pluginManager clientmgmt.Manager, logger logrus.FieldLogger) (interface{}, error) {
	return f.backupStores[location.Name], nil
}

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Testing BSL Controller with Metrics Integration:")
	
	// Setup
	velerov1api.AddToScheme(scheme.Scheme)
	
	pluginManager := &pluginmocks.Manager{}
	pluginManager.On("CleanupClients").Return(nil)
	
	// Create test BSL locations
	locationAvailable := builder.ForBackupStorageLocation("ns-1", "location-available").
		ValidationFrequency(1 * time.Second).
		Default(true).
		Result()
	
	locationUnavailable := builder.ForBackupStorageLocation("ns-1", "location-unavailable").
		ValidationFrequency(1 * time.Second).
		Result()
	
	locations := &velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList{
		Items: []velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation{*locationAvailable, *locationUnavailable},
	}
	
	// Create mock backup stores
	backupStores := make(map[string]*persistencemocks.BackupStore)
	backupStores["location-available"] = &persistencemocks.BackupStore{}
	backupStores["location-available"].On("IsValid").Return(nil) // Valid
	
	backupStores["location-unavailable"] = &persistencemocks.BackupStore{}
	backupStores["location-unavailable"].On("IsValid").Return(fmt.Errorf("invalid storage")) // Invalid
	
	// Create metrics
	serverMetrics := metrics.NewServerMetrics()
	
	// Create reconciler with metrics
	r := &controller.BackupStorageLocationReconciler{
		Ctx:    context.Background(),
		Client: fake.NewClientBuilder().WithScheme(scheme.Scheme).WithRuntimeObjects(locations).Build(),
		DefaultBackupLocationInfo: storage.DefaultBackupLocationInfo{
			StorageLocation:           "location-available",
			ServerValidationFrequency: 0,
		},
		NewPluginManager:  func(logrus.FieldLogger) clientmgmt.Manager { return pluginManager },
		BackupStoreGetter: NewFakeObjectBackupStoreGetter(backupStores),
		Metrics:           serverMetrics,
		Log:               logrus.New(),
	}
	
	// Reconcile the available location
	fmt.Println("\n1. Reconciling Available BSL:")
	result, err := r.Reconcile(context.Background(), ctrl.Request{
		NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{Namespace: "ns-1", Name: "location-available"},
	})
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("  Error: %v\n", err)
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("  Result: %v\n", result)
		fmt.Println("  ✓ Available BSL reconciled successfully")
	}
	
	// Reconcile the unavailable location
	fmt.Println("\n2. Reconciling Unavailable BSL:")
	result, err = r.Reconcile(context.Background(), ctrl.Request{
		NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{Namespace: "ns-1", Name: "location-unavailable"},
	})
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("  Error: %v\n", err)
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("  Result: %v\n", result)
		fmt.Println("  ✓ Unavailable BSL reconciled successfully")
	}
	
	// Verify BSL status in the client
	fmt.Println("\n3. Verifying BSL statuses:")
	
	var locAvailable velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
	err = r.Client.Get(context.Background(), types.NamespacedName{Namespace: "ns-1", Name: "location-available"}, &locAvailable)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("  Error getting available location: %v\n", err)
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("  Available Location Phase: %s\n", locAvailable.Status.Phase)
		if locAvailable.Status.Phase == velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseAvailable {
			fmt.Println("  ✓ Available location has correct phase")
		}
	}
	
	var locUnavailable velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
	err = r.Client.Get(context.Background(), types.NamespacedName{Namespace: "ns-1", Name: "location-unavailable"}, &locUnavailable)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("  Error getting unavailable location: %v\n", err)
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("  Unavailable Location Phase: %s\n", locUnavailable.Status.Phase)
		if locUnavailable.Status.Phase == velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseUnavailable {
			fmt.Println("  ✓ Unavailable location has correct phase")
		}
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\n✓ All integration tests passed!")
}

	// Test changing status
	fmt.Println("\n3. Testing status change:")
	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-changing", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Println("   Set BSL '"'"'test-bsl-changing'"'"' to Available")
	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-changing", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	fmt.Println("   Changed BSL '"'"'test-bsl-changing'"'"' to Unavailable")
	fmt.Println("   ✓ Status change successful")
	
	// Verify constants
	fmt.Println("\n4. Verifying metric constants:")
	fmt.Printf("   BSLLastStatusAvailable = %d (expected: 1)\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Printf("   BSLLastStatusUnavailable = %d (expected: 0)\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	
	if metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable == 1 && metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable == 0 {
		fmt.Println("   ✓ Constants are correct")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("   ✗ Constants are incorrect")
		return
	}
	
	// Verify that the constants match the backup constants pattern
	fmt.Println("\n5. Comparing with Backup metrics pattern:")
	fmt.Printf("   BackupLastStatusSucc = %d\n", metrics.BackupLastStatusSucc)
	fmt.Printf("   BackupLastStatusFailure = %d\n", metrics.BackupLastStatusFailure)
	fmt.Printf("   BSLLastStatusAvailable = %d\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Printf("   BSLLastStatusUnavailable = %d\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	
	if metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable == metrics.BackupLastStatusSucc && 
	   metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable == metrics.BackupLastStatusFailure {
		fmt.Println("   ✓ BSL metrics follow the same pattern as Backup metrics")
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\n=================================")
	fmt.Println("✓ All tests passed successfully!")
	fmt.Println("=================================")
}

	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-available", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Printf("   Set BSL '"'"'test-bsl-available'"'"' to Available (value: %d)\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Println("   ✓ Method called successfully")
	
	// Test setting to unavailable
	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-unavailable", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	fmt.Printf("   Set BSL '"'"'test-bsl-unavailable'"'"' to Unavailable (value: %d)\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	fmt.Println("   ✓ Method called successfully")
	
	// Test changing status
	fmt.Println("\n3. Testing status change:")
	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-changing", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Println("   Set BSL '"'"'test-bsl-changing'"'"' to Available")
	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-changing", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	fmt.Println("   Changed BSL '"'"'test-bsl-changing'"'"' to Unavailable")
	fmt.Println("   ✓ Status change successful")
	
	// Verify constants
	fmt.Println("\n4. Verifying metric constants:")
	fmt.Printf("   BSLLastStatusAvailable = %d (expected: 1)\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Printf("   BSLLastStatusUnavailable = %d (expected: 0)\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	
	if metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable == 1 && metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable == 0 {
		fmt.Println("   ✓ Constants are correct")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("   ✗ Constants are incorrect")
		return
	}
	
	// Verify that the constants match the backup constants pattern
	fmt.Println("\n5. Comparing with Backup metrics pattern:")
	fmt.Printf("   BackupLastStatusSucc = %d\n", metrics.BackupLastStatusSucc)
	fmt.Printf("   BackupLastStatusFailure = %d\n", metrics.BackupLastStatusFailure)
	fmt.Printf("   BSLLastStatusAvailable = %d\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Printf("   BSLLastStatusUnavailable = %d\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	
	if metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable == metrics.BackupLastStatusSucc && 
	   metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable == metrics.BackupLastStatusFailure {
		fmt.Println("   ✓ BSL metrics follow the same pattern as Backup metrics")
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\n=================================")
	fmt.Println("✓ All tests passed successfully!")
	fmt.Println("=================================")

	"fmt"

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Testing BSL Metrics Integration:")

	fmt.Printf("   Set BSL '"'"'test-bsl-available'"'"' to Available (value: %d)\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Println("   ✓ Method called successfully")
	
	// Test setting to unavailable
	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-unavailable", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	fmt.Printf("   Set BSL '"'"'test-bsl-unavailable'"'"' to Unavailable (value: %d)\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	fmt.Println("   ✓ Method called successfully")
	
	// Test changing status
	fmt.Println("\n3. Testing status change:")
	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-changing", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Println("   Set BSL '"'"'test-bsl-changing'"'"' to Available")
	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-changing", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	fmt.Println("   Changed BSL '"'"'test-bsl-changing'"'"' to Unavailable")
	fmt.Println("   ✓ Status change successful")
	
	// Verify constants
	fmt.Println("\n4. Verifying metric constants:")
	fmt.Printf("   BSLLastStatusAvailable = %d (expected: 1)\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Printf("   BSLLastStatusUnavailable = %d (expected: 0)\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	
	if metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable == 1 && metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable == 0 {
		fmt.Println("   ✓ Constants are correct")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("   ✗ Constants are incorrect")
		return
	}
	
	// Verify that the constants match the backup constants pattern
	fmt.Println("\n5. Comparing with Backup metrics pattern:")
	fmt.Printf("   BackupLastStatusSucc = %d\n", metrics.BackupLastStatusSucc)
	fmt.Printf("   BackupLastStatusFailure = %d\n", metrics.BackupLastStatusFailure)
	fmt.Printf("   BSLLastStatusAvailable = %d\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Printf("   BSLLastStatusUnavailable = %d\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)

	   metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable == metrics.BackupLastStatusFailure {
		fmt.Println("   ✓ BSL metrics follow the same pattern as Backup metrics")
	}

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"

	"github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pkg/metrics"
)

// This test demonstrates the new BSL metrics feature
func main() {
	fmt.Println("====================================================")
	fmt.Println("BSL Metrics Feature Demonstration")
	fmt.Println("====================================================")
	
	// Test 1: Create metrics instance
	fmt.Println("\n[Test 1] Creating ServerMetrics instance...")
	serverMetrics := metrics.NewServerMetrics()
	if serverMetrics == nil {
		fmt.Println("❌ FAILED: Could not create ServerMetrics")
		os.Exit(1)
	}
	fmt.Println("✅ PASSED: ServerMetrics instance created")
	
	// Test 2: Verify constants are properly defined
	fmt.Println("\n[Test 2] Verifying BSL status constants...")
	if metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable != 1 {
		fmt.Printf("❌ FAILED: BSLLastStatusAvailable = %d, expected 1\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
		os.Exit(1)
	}
	if metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable != 0 {
		fmt.Printf("❌ FAILED: BSLLastStatusUnavailable = %d, expected 0\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
		os.Exit(1)
	}
	fmt.Println("✅ PASSED: BSL status constants are correct")
	fmt.Printf("   - BSLLastStatusAvailable = %d\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Printf("   - BSLLastStatusUnavailable = %d\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	
	// Test 3: Test setting BSL status to Available
	fmt.Println("\n[Test 3] Setting BSL status to Available...")
	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-1", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Println("✅ PASSED: Successfully set BSL '"'"'test-bsl-1'"'"' to Available")
	
	// Test 4: Test setting BSL status to Unavailable
	fmt.Println("\n[Test 4] Setting BSL status to Unavailable...")
	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-2", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	fmt.Println("✅ PASSED: Successfully set BSL '"'"'test-bsl-2'"'"' to Unavailable")
	
	// Test 5: Test changing BSL status
	fmt.Println("\n[Test 5] Testing status change...")
	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-3", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)
	fmt.Println("   - Set BSL '"'"'test-bsl-3'"'"' to Available")
	serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus("test-bsl-3", metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	fmt.Println("   - Changed BSL '"'"'test-bsl-3'"'"' to Unavailable")
	fmt.Println("✅ PASSED: Status change works correctly")
	
	// Test 6: Test multiple BSLs
	fmt.Println("\n[Test 6] Testing multiple BSLs...")
	bslNames := []string{"default", "aws-backup", "azure-backup", "gcp-backup"}
	for i, name := range bslNames {
		status := metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable
		if i%2 == 1 {
			status = metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable
		}
		serverMetrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus(name, status)
		statusStr := "Available"
		if status == metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable {
			statusStr = "Unavailable"
		}
		fmt.Printf("   - Set BSL '"'"'%s'"'"' to %s\n", name, statusStr)
	}
	fmt.Println("✅ PASSED: Multiple BSLs handled correctly")
	
	// Test 7: Verify pattern consistency with backup metrics
	fmt.Println("\n[Test 7] Verifying consistency with backup metrics pattern...")
	if metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable != metrics.BackupLastStatusSucc {
		fmt.Println("❌ FAILED: BSL Available doesn'"'"'t match Backup Success pattern")
		os.Exit(1)
	}
	if metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable != metrics.BackupLastStatusFailure {
		fmt.Println("❌ FAILED: BSL Unavailable doesn'"'"'t match Backup Failure pattern")
		os.Exit(1)
	}
	fmt.Println("✅ PASSED: BSL metrics follow the same pattern as backup metrics")
	fmt.Printf("   - Backup: Success=%d, Failure=%d\n", metrics.BackupLastStatusSucc, metrics.BackupLastStatusFailure)
	fmt.Printf("   - BSL: Available=%d, Unavailable=%d\n", metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable, metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)
	
	fmt.Println("\n====================================================")
	fmt.Println("✅ ALL TESTS PASSED!")
	fmt.Println("====================================================")
	fmt.Println("\nMetric Details:")
	fmt.Println("---------------")
	fmt.Println("Metric Name: velero_backup_storage_location_last_status")
	fmt.Println("Metric Type: Gauge")
	fmt.Println("Label: backupStorageLocation")
	fmt.Println("Values:")
	fmt.Println("  - 1: BSL is Available (valid)")
	fmt.Println("  - 0: BSL is Unavailable (invalid)")
	fmt.Println("\nExample Usage in Prometheus:")
	fmt.Println("  velero_backup_storage_location_last_status{backupStorageLocation=\"default\"}")
	fmt.Println()
}
'

str_replace_editor create /testbed/IMPLEMENTATION_SUMMARY.md --file_text '# BSL Metrics Implementation Summary

## Overview
This implementation adds a new metric for Backup Storage Location (BSL) to show whether the BSL is valid or invalid, as requested in the PR description.

## Changes Made

### 1. Metrics Package (`/testbed/pkg/metrics/metrics.go`)

#### Added Constants:
- `backupStorageLocationLastStatus = "backup_storage_location_last_status"` - Metric name constant
- `bslNameLabel = "backupStorageLocation"` - Label name for BSL identification
- `BSLLastStatusAvailable int64 = 1` - Value for available/valid BSL
- `BSLLastStatusUnavailable int64 = 0` - Value for unavailable/invalid BSL

#### Added Metric Definition:
In `NewServerMetrics()` function, registered a new GaugeVec metric:
```go
backupStorageLocationLastStatus: prometheus.NewGaugeVec(
    prometheus.GaugeOpts{
        Namespace: metricNamespace,
        Name:      backupStorageLocationLastStatus,
        Help:      "Last status of the backup storage location. A value of 1 is available, 0 is unavailable",
    },
    []string{bslNameLabel},
),
```

#### Added Method:
```go
func (m *ServerMetrics) SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus(bslName string, lastStatus int64) {
    if g, ok := m.metrics[backupStorageLocationLastStatus].(*prometheus.GaugeVec); ok {
        g.WithLabelValues(bslName).Set(float64(lastStatus))
    }
}
```

### 2. BSL Controller (`/testbed/pkg/controller/backup_storage_location_controller.go`)

#### Modified Struct:
Added `metrics *metrics.ServerMetrics` field to `backupStorageLocationReconciler` struct.

#### Modified Constructor:
Updated `NewBackupStorageLocationReconciler()` to accept a `metrics *metrics.ServerMetrics` parameter.

#### Modified Reconcile Logic:
In the `Reconcile()` method, added metric updates when BSL status changes:
- When BSL is valid/available: `r.metrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus(location.Name, metrics.BSLLastStatusAvailable)`
- When BSL is invalid/unavailable: `r.metrics.SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus(location.Name, metrics.BSLLastStatusUnavailable)`

### 3. Server Initialization (`/testbed/pkg/cmd/server/server.go`)

#### Modified BSL Controller Initialization:
Updated the call to `NewBackupStorageLocationReconciler()` to pass the metrics instance:
```go
bslr := controller.NewBackupStorageLocationReconciler(
    s.ctx,
    s.mgr.GetClient(),
    storage.DefaultBackupLocationInfo{
        StorageLocation:           s.config.DefaultBackupLocation,
        ServerValidationFrequency: s.config.StoreValidationFrequency,
    },
    newPluginManager,
    backupStoreGetter,
    s.metrics,  // <-- Added this parameter
    s.logger,
)
```

### 4. Test Files (`/testbed/pkg/controller/backup_storage_location_controller_test.go`)

#### Updated Test Instances:
Added `metrics: nil` field to all test instances of `backupStorageLocationReconciler` to maintain compatibility with the new struct definition.

## Metric Specification

### Metric Name
`velero_backup_storage_location_last_status`

### Metric Type
Gauge

### Labels
- `backupStorageLocation`: The name of the BSL

### Values
- `1`: BSL is Available (valid/accessible)
- `0`: BSL is Unavailable (invalid/inaccessible)

### Example Prometheus Queries
```promql
# Get status of all BSLs
velero_backup_storage_location_last_status

# Get status of a specific BSL
velero_backup_storage_location_last_status{backupStorageLocation="default"}

# Count unavailable BSLs
count(velero_backup_storage_location_last_status == 0)

# Alert when any BSL becomes unavailable
velero_backup_storage_location_last_status == 0
```

## Behavior

The metric is automatically updated whenever the BSL controller validates a BSL:
1. During BSL validation, the controller checks if the backup store is valid
2. If validation succeeds, the metric is set to `1` (Available)
3. If validation fails, the metric is set to `0` (Unavailable)
4. The metric persists until the next validation cycle

## Pattern Consistency

The implementation follows the same pattern as the existing `backup_last_status` metric:
- Both use Gauge metrics
- Both use binary values (1 for success/available, 0 for failure/unavailable)
- Both update automatically during reconciliation
- Both support multiple instances via labels

## Testing

All code compiles successfully:
- ✅ `pkg/metrics` package builds without errors
- ✅ `pkg/controller` package builds without errors
- ✅ `pkg/cmd/server` package builds without errors
- ✅ Existing tests updated and compatible
- ✅ Metric constants are properly defined
- ✅ Method works correctly with different BSL names

## Edge Cases Handled

1. **Nil Metrics**: The controller checks if `r.metrics != nil` before calling the metric method, ensuring no panics if metrics are not initialized (useful for testing)
2. **Multiple BSLs**: Each BSL gets its own metric instance with a unique label value
3. **Status Changes**: The metric correctly updates when a BSL transitions between available and unavailable states
4. **Concurrent BSLs**: The label-based approach supports multiple BSLs being validated concurrently

## Future Enhancements (Out of Scope)

Potential future improvements that could build on this implementation:
- Add a metric for validation frequency/timing
- Add metrics for BSL sync operations
- Add metrics for BSL access mode changes
- Add a histogram for validation duration

+// SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus records the last status of the backup storage location.
+func (m *ServerMetrics) SetBackupStorageLocationLastStatus(bslName string, lastStatus int64) {
+	if g, ok := m.metrics[backupStorageLocationLastStatus].(*prometheus.GaugeVec); ok {
+		g.WithLabelValues(bslName).Set(float64(lastStatus))
+	}
+}
